## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |

| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# ClickHouse Access Control and Row-Level Security Policy Audit

## Your Task

Audit the access control and row-level security implementation in ClickHouse/ClickHouse. Find all C++ source and header files under src/Access/ that implement: the AccessControl manager and its user/role resolution, the RowPolicy filter generation and attachment to queries, the ContextAccess class that checks permissions per query, the IAccessStorage interface hierarchy (UsersConfigAccessStorage, DiskAccessStorage, ReplicatedAccessStorage), and the GRANT/REVOKE statement handlers. Report each file path and key class.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the security domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/ClickHouse--v24.12.

## Output Format

Create a file at `/workspace/answer.json` with your findings in the following structure:

```json
{
  "files": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go"}
  ],
  "symbols": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go", "symbol": "SymbolName"}
  ],
  "chain": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go", "symbol": "FunctionName"}
  ],
  "text": "Narrative explanation of your findings, citing repos and file paths."
}
```

Include only the fields relevant to this task. Your answer is evaluated against a closed-world oracle — completeness matters.

## Evaluation

Your answer will be scored on:
- **File recall and precision**: Did you find all relevant files?

68-assistanttext-
Perfect! I've completed a comprehensive audit of the ClickHouse access control and row-level security implementation. The results have been written to `/workspace/answer.json`.

## Summary

I've identified and documented **41 key files** and **21 critical classes** implementing ClickHouse's access control system:

### Key Components Audited:

1. **AccessControl Manager** - Central hub managing multiple access storages, caching, and subscriptions
2. **User/Role Resolution** - User and Role classes with access rights, granted roles, and authentication data
3. **ContextAccess** - Per-query permission checking with access validation and row policy application
4. **RowPolicy System** - Filter generation and attachment through RowPolicyCache and EnabledRowPolicies
5. **IAccessStorage Hierarchy** - 6 implementations covering users.xml, disk persistence, ZooKeeper replication, memory storage, LDAP, and multi-storage management
6. **GRANT/REVOKE Handlers** - InterpreterGrantQuery for statement execution, plus CHECK GRANT and SHOW GRANTS support
7. **Supporting Infrastructure** - Role caching, access rights trees, quota management, and change notifications

All files are located in `src/Access/` and `src/Interpreters/Access/` directories with both `.h` (header) and `.cpp` (implementation) files for each major component.

It:\\n- Checks if a specified access (read, write, admin) is granted (checkAccess methods)\\n- Checks grant options for permission delegation (checkGrantOption methods)\\n- Returns row policy filters for table access control (getRowPolicyFilter)\\n- Manages quota tracking (getQuota)\\n- Returns enabled roles and default settings\\n- Supports admin option checking for role delegation\\nContextAccess is created via AccessControl.getContextAccess() with ContextAccessParams (src/Access/ContextAccessParams.h/cpp)\\n\\nROW-LEVEL SECURITY (ROW POLICY) IMPLEMENTATION:\\nRow policies are defined in src/Access/RowPolicy.h as access entities with:\\n- Filter expressions for different operations (SELECT, INSERT, UPDATE, DELETE)\\n- Permissive vs. restrictive modes\\n- Application to specific roles or users (RolesOrUsersSet)\\n- Support for database-level or table-level policies\\n\\nRow policy filter generation and attachment:\\n- RowPolicyCache (src/Access/RowPolicyCache.h/cpp) - stores, parses, and caches row policies\\n- EnabledRowPolicies (src/Access/EnabledRowPolicies.h/cpp) - provides fast access to row policy filters for a user\\n- Filters are retrieved via ContextAccess.getRowPolicyFilter(database, table, filter_type)\\n- RowPolicyFilter (defined in EnabledRowPolicies.h) contains the parsed AST expression and combining logic\\n\\nIACCESSSSTORAGE INTERFACE HIERARCHY:\\nAll access entity storages implement the IAccessStorage interface (src/Access/IAccessStorage.h/cpp), which defines:\\n- find, read, insert, remove, update operations for access entities\\n- Authentication handling (authenticate method)\\n- Backup and restore functionality\\n\\nImplementations:\\n1. UsersConfigAccessStorage (src/Access/UsersConfigAccessStorage.h/cpp) - reads users from users.xml configuration file (read-only)\\n2. DiskAccessStorage (src/Access/DiskAccessStorage.h/cpp) - persists access entities to local disk in a directory structure, supports background list writing\\n3. ReplicatedAccessStorage (src/Access/ReplicatedAccessStorage.h/cpp) - stores access entities in ZooKeeper for cluster-wide replication\\n4. MemoryAccessStorage (src/Access/MemoryAccessStorage.h/cpp) - in-memory storage for temporary or testing use\\n5. MultipleAccessStorage (src/Access/MultipleAccessStorage.h/cpp) - manages multiple nested storages with priority/lookup\\n6. LDAPAccessStorage (src/Access/LDAPAccessStorage.h/cpp) - authenticates users against external LDAP servers\\n\\nACCESS RIGHTS MANAGEMENT:\\nAccessRights class (src/Access/AccessRights.h/cpp) represents granted access types with:\\n- Grant operations at global, database, table, and column levels\\n- Support for grant options (WITH GRANT OPTION)\\n- Wildcard grants for matching multiple entities\\n- Revoke operations with similar granularity\\n- Intersection, union, and difference operations for combining rights from multiple roles\\n\\nGRANT/REVOKE STATEMENT HANDLERS:\\nThe GRANT and REVOKE SQL statements are handled through:\\n- InterpreterGrantQuery (src/Interpreters/Access/InterpreterGrantQuery.h/cpp) - executes GRANT/REVOKE statements and updates User/Role objects via updateUserFromQuery() and updateRoleFromQuery() methods\\n- InterpreterCheckGrantQuery (src/Interpreters/Access/InterpreterCheckGrantQuery.h/cpp) - implements CHECK GRANT statements to verify permissions\\n- InterpreterShowGrantsQuery (src/Interpreters/Access/InterpreterShowGrantsQuery.h/cpp) - displays current grants for users/roles\\n\\nADDITIONAL SUPPORTING COMPONENTS:\\n- AccessChangesNotifier (src/Access/AccessChangesNotifier.h/cpp) - notifies dependent caches when access entities change\\n- ContextAccessParams (src/Access/ContextAccessParams.h/cpp) - contains parameters for creating ContextAccess instances\\n- EnabledRolesInfo - stores resolved roles and their access rights\\n- RolesOrUsersSet - represents sets of roles or users for policy application\\n\\nThe architecture follows a hierarchical cache model: AccessControl -> RoleCache/RowPolicyCache/ContextAccessCache -> EnabledRoles/EnabledRowPolicies/ContextAccess, with subscription-based invalidation when entities change.\"\n}\n",

(src/Access/AccessControl.h/cpp) is the central manager for the access control system. The AccessControl manager is responsible for:\\n- Managing multiple access storage implementations\\n- User/role resolution through getContextAccess(), getEnabledRoles(), and getEnabledRolesInfo()\\n- Caching mechanisms: ContextAccessCache, RoleCache, RowPolicyCache, QuotaCache, SettingsProfilesCache\\n- Configuration management and reload operations\\n- Subscription management for access entity changes through AccessChangesNotifier\\n\\nUSER AND ROLE RESOLUTION:\\nUsers are defined in src/Access/User.h as an access entity containing:\\n- Authentication methods (AuthenticationData)\\n- Access rights (AccessRights)\\n- Granted roles (GrantedRoles)\\n- Default roles (RolesOrUsersSet)\\n- Settings profiles\\n- Allowed client hosts\\n\\nRoles are defined in src/Access/Role.h containing:\\n- Access rights (AccessRights)\\n- Granted roles (GrantedRoles) - roles can grant other roles\\n- Settings profiles\\n\\nRole resolution is handled by:\\n- RoleCache (src/Access/RoleCache.h/cpp) - caches and resolves enabled roles with expiration\\n- EnabledRoles (src/Access/EnabledRoles.h/cpp) - represents current roles for a session\\n- GrantedRoles (src/Access/GrantedRoles.h/cpp) - tracks both regular roles and roles with admin option\\n\\nCONTEXTACCESS PERMISSION CHECKING:\\nThe ContextAccess class (src/Access/ContextAccess.h/cpp) implements per-query permission checking. It:\\n- Checks if a specified access (read, write, admin) is granted (checkAccess methods)\\n- Checks grant options for permission delegation (checkGrantOption methods)\\n- Returns row policy filters for table access control (getRowPolicyFilter)\\n- Manages quota tracking (getQuota)\\n- Returns enabled roles and default settings\\n- Supports admin option checking for role delegation\\nContextAccess is created via AccessControl.getContextAccess() with ContextAccessParams (src/Access/ContextAccessParams.h/cpp)\\n\\nROW-LEVEL SECURITY (ROW POLICY) IMPLEMENTATION:\\nRow policies are defined in src/Access/RowPolicy.h as access entities with:\\n- Filter expressions for different operations (SELECT, INSERT, UPDATE, DELETE)\\n- Permissive vs. restrictive modes\\n- Application to specific roles or users (RolesOrUsersSet)\\n- Support for database-level or table-level policies\\n\\nRow policy filter generation and attachment:\\n- RowPolicyCache (src/Access/RowPolicyCache.h/cpp) - stores, parses, and caches row policies\\n- EnabledRowPolicies (src/Access/EnabledRowPolicies.h/cpp) - provides fast access to row policy filters for a user\\n- Filters are retrieved via ContextAccess.getRowPolicyFilter(database, table, filter_type)\\n- RowPolicyFilter (defined in EnabledRowPolicies.h) contains the parsed AST expression and combining logic\\n\\nIACCESSSSTORAGE INTERFACE HIERARCHY:\\nAll access entity storages implement the IAccessStorage interface (src/Access/IAccessStorage.h/cpp), which defines:\\n- find, read, insert, remove, update operations for access entities\\n- Authentication handling (authenticate method)\\n- Backup and restore functionality\\n\\nImplementations:\\n1. UsersConfigAccessStorage (src/Access/UsersConfigAccessStorage.h/cpp) - reads users from users.xml configuration file (read-only)\\n2. DiskAccessStorage (src/Access/DiskAccessStorage.h/cpp) - persists access entities to local disk in a directory structure, supports background list writing\\n3. ReplicatedAccessStorage (src/Access/ReplicatedAccessStorage.h/cpp) - stores access entities in ZooKeeper for cluster-wide replication\\n4. MemoryAccessStorage (src/Access/MemoryAccessStorage.h/cpp) - in-memory storage for temporary or testing use\\n5. MultipleAccessStorage (src/Access/MultipleAccessStorage.h/cpp) - manages multiple nested storages with priority/lookup\\n6. LDAPAccessStorage (src/Access/LDAPAccessStorage.h/cpp) - authenticates users against external LDAP servers\\n\\nACCESS RIGHTS MANAGEMENT:\\nAccessRights class (src/Access/AccessRights.h/cpp) represents granted access types with:\\n- Grant operations at global, database, table, and column levels\\n- Support for grant options (WITH GRANT OPTION)\\n- Wildcard grants for matching multiple entities\\n- Revoke operations with similar granularity\\n- Intersection, union, and difference operations for combining rights from multiple roles\\n\\nGRANT/REVOKE STATEMENT HANDLERS:\\nThe GRANT and REVOKE SQL statements are handled through:\\n- InterpreterGrantQuery (src/Interpreters/Access/InterpreterGrantQuery.h/cpp) - executes GRANT/REVOKE statements and updates User/Role objects via updateUserFromQuery() and updateRoleFromQuery() methods\\n- InterpreterCheckGrantQuery (src/Interpreters/Access/InterpreterCheckGrantQuery.h/cpp) - implements CHECK GRANT statements to verify permissions\\n- InterpreterShowGrantsQuery (src/Interpreters/Access/InterpreterShowGrantsQuery.h/cpp) - displays current grants for users/roles\\n\\nADDITIONAL SUPPORTING COMPONENTS:\\n- AccessChangesNotifier (src/Access/AccessChangesNotifier.h/cpp) - notifies dependent caches when access entities change\\n- ContextAccessParams (src/Access/ContextAccessParams.h/cpp) - contains parameters for creating ContextAccess instances\\n- EnabledRolesInfo - stores resolved roles and their access rights\\n- RolesOrUsersSet - represents sets of roles or users for policy application\\n\\nThe architecture follows a hierarchical cache model: AccessControl -> RoleCache/RowPolicyCache/ContextAccessCache -> EnabledRoles/EnabledRowPolicies/ContextAccess, with subscription-based invalidation when entities change.\"\n}\n",
